My husband & i wish to warn anyone who will read reviews before picking a vet. Do not pick Dr. Deoul. I wish I did not have to put any star. Our experience is horrific. We brought our two cocker spaniels in for an annual blood panel and vaccinations. A well check up. We received a great report on their blood. Our dogs have never been sick in their 8.5 years of life. Very healthy.  We were very disappointed on arriving the doctor did not even come into the room to greet us. A young staff gal led us to room & suggested it would all go faster if she could take dogs one by one to back room for exam, blood draw & vaccinations. Kind of surprised we wouldn‚Äôt even see the Dr. Deoul? Figured we would see him when all was completed? Never saw him. Was led to front desk and given invoice for over $600! A bit shocked, but asked when we know blood results? Receptionist called with good blood results. Two days later our horror began. One of our cockers had a deathly reaction to the DA2PP Vaccination. She literally was dying before our eyes. We called office & was told CASUALLY if we like we could bring her in. If we like?! She had stopped eating, feverish, not drinking totally listless. We were casually brought into private room. Expecting the doctor? Receptionist returns to tell (no doctor) us they will need to draw more blood & it will cost approx $270! Receptionist tells us she would take our cocker to back room (still no doc). We were told to leave & return later for these blood results. We did, FINALLY first time we see doctor! almost $800 later and our Zoe sicker than ever. Tells us she had autoimmune reaction to vaccine, gave her a couple meds after a shot & hydrated her. He felt though her blood count went from 58 to 18, she did not need a blood transfusion. Quickly told by receptionist this bill will be $407! Omg! Along with meds to give her. Doc said if she gets worse over night call him. Returning home we noticed bright red blood after she urinated. Shocked I called office doc said IF WE LIKE could return her for a blood clotting blood test. Of course we did so! She was completely healthy before this vet. $179 after blood clotting test was told take her home the test seemed fine, & call if she got worse with yellowing in mouth & ears. I asked for a discount on invoice being that she was in perfect health, proved by her blood work up two days before, & it was their vaccination that caused it all. Of course, they are money hungry, not animal lovers, no discount because it was due to her immune response. No mercy! She was extremely yellow next am, no longer could walk, called doctor office left msg, no answer. Sent email, no response. Broken hearted we left for another vet who was awesome! She could not believe within 2 days her blood count went from 58 to 18 & Dr Deoul felt no transfusion was necessary. New vet said if blood had fallen that fast in a couple days, going another evening it surely had dropped more. She immediately got us into VCA EMERGENCY Hospital. She is now in critical condition, had a transfusion, but she‚Äôs in God‚Äôs hands working thru physicians there.  My son had horrible experience several years ago with their pug & Dr Deoul. They said NO REFUND. If you love your pet - go elsewhere. All they care about is money! No compassion, no mercy, no love. It‚Äôs been twelve hours since our last call to Dr Deoul who has never returned our call or email. Not even to ask how precious little Zoey is. I‚Äôm sure he figures she‚Äôs dead and can‚Äôt get anymore money out of us.  Very sad. He and his staff our not meant to care for our loved ones.

< Date>
1557451953510</Date>
<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Took my Fender Jazz in to get a Plek'd setup for drop C with D'Addario XL 105's. The job required a new neck, as the old neck had warped too badly to be setup, but they called and told me about the additional cost before replacing it. The new neck feels amazing, the action is so much better, and there's no fret buzz at all on any of the low frets, even given the low tuning I use. Be sure to mention the tuning you'll be playing in when you bring you instrument in, as I didn't, and they needed to re-adjust the truss-rod quickly when I picked it (which they were hapopy to do), as they had set it up for standard tuning. They did a great job, I highly recommend them.</Review>

<Text>Sometimes you just get lucky.
I found Hugh and 13th Street Guitars looking for a used guitar on Craigslist.  When I went to check it out, I ran into 3 customers at the store.  Making small talk, I was blown away at what everyone was saying about the owner, Hugh.  They speak of him like a guitar wizard, capable of turning a kit guitar into a Martin.  It was just like the other reviews that I read online.  One of the customers even haggled with Hugh on the price...but not to pay less, to pay more!  I knew I found the right place.
I'm new to the guitar, so I didn't really know how important a good set up was.  The guitar I bought had a full set up from Hugh upon purchase.  But since playing my guitar for sometime now, and subsequently playing other guitars not set up by Hugh...even more expensive guitars not set up by Hugh, I'm convinced of his wizardry.
He also happens to be a kind person and is easy to communicate with (which sadly is worth noting in todays day and age).

{'time': 1602306881973, 'text': 'Ciao Samantha, what a nice review. Thanks so much, it really means a lot to us when a customer is so loyal and nice to us. I think it is the best part of my job to interact with people who like what we do!!\nSince you like the Rose, a little story for you. We use a rose extract to make it, a very gourmet product prepared on purpose for gelato. We make a custom recipe with a little beet powder (natural colorants is all we use for color) and what comes out is the pale pastel pink, delicate and aromatic flavor you know.\nOne day we were producing a very big batch for a wholesale order (we supply many restaurants around the Bay Area). At the moment of the extraction the gelato came out bright fucsia. It was unnaturally saturated and so full of color it seemed almost impossible to compare to our usual delicate pink. We checked the recipe, the ingredients, possible balance mistake but all seemed in place... So we contacted the producer, a big respectable Italian company, to complain. It turned out that the change was made on purpose!! The biggest consumer of Rose gelato is Saudi Arabia where gelato is very trendy at the moment. They apparently like their Rose neon bright Pink!! It was a disaster, we had to look for another supplier, modify and balance the recipe and we got back to our usual sweet delicate delicacy! I am so glad you like it and I hope you might be back to Berkeley soon to taste it again, maybe combined with Cardamom Custard, an amazing combo... Thanks for your support and nice words. < text>
The people that work here are extremely friendly and very helpful-- very nice people.  The gelato is absolutely spectacular.  The best gelato I have ever had!  The flavors are extraordinary, and like nothing you would find in a normal ice cream shop.  I had a raspberry flavor-- it tasted like there were real fresh raspberries in it! This place rocks.

Not to mention their hot chocolate was thickly amazing-- it was like the whole drink was just a rich, melted chunk of chocolate.

Go here!  It really is great.</text>

< username>
Lea S<//username>
< Pics>
None</Pics>
<rating>4< /rating><Resp>None</Resp><gmapID>0x80857e9c353d06f1:0x2d598dbb360efcc9</gmapID>< Review>
You will find this place just outside the BART station. Very convenient if you come from a long ride and want something cold and refreshing. The place is really small (take the ice cream and go eat it outside, there are only three or four tables if I'm not mistaken), but has what you've come for - gelato. A proper gelato. The staff is friendly and patient, even if you have a hard time deciding (and you will have a hard time deciding).

They have different tastes (I can't for the love of god remember how many they had last weekend, when I was there, but I'd say at least 16 different ones). They also have a sign outside of their establishment that will tell you the "specials" for the season. I'll have to come again to see how they change.

I ordered rose, vanilla and pistachio. All three were really good! You can have them in a cone or in a cup (better choice, if you don't want to get all "ice creamy"). The price is by the amount of scoops you'll have and it's pricey, yes (this is Berkeley, don't forget that), but then again, it is a very tasty gelato.

They also offer hot chocolate, coffee, tea and some other nuts and chocolate, if you're not into ice cream, but that's not the point.

Will come back for more, for sure. :)< /Review>

Did my research, and decided to purchase the Hercules 12" Sliding Compound Miter Saw with the Hercules Stand. I've read quite a few reviews, and decided that for my level of use, I should be satisfied for the price. I looked at the Dewalt...but was more that I wanted to pay. I'm going to purchase the Hercules 80 teeth blade for doing fine cutting in the future. Plan on getting more items later. By the way, Thanks  to John the Manager. < Text>
I'm so quick to complain and sometimes don't give kudos to those whom deserve them.
Not long ago, I posted a negative post about Harbor Fright of Hanford. I've since visited the store countless times. It's a big toy store to me.

I can't help myself, the prices are great!  The coupons to save on an already on sale item.  Super Savings. I am lame, I'll admit, again I couldn't find an item.  I asked as Associate to assistance and he took me to every item on my list.
The kind of service an associate wants to provide,  loves the job so much that it to the Associate, seems effortless.  I thank the Associate that helped me.
The counter Associates are very patient, supper helpful and friendly

We all have bad days. I regret the things said in an earlier post. Me having a bad day.  Please forgive me for any inconvenience I may have caused.
It's so good to have Harbor Freight in our Community.

Thank you Harbor Freight.

Best Regards,
